# `ssa-nomerge` Binaryen Parity

This page is the current local signoff tracker.
Use the strategy and shape pages in this folder for the upstream Binaryen algorithm itself; use `[./implementation-structure-and-tests.md](./implementation-structure-and-tests.md)` for owner-file and proof-surface navigation. This page is about the repo's current evidence and remaining gaps.

## Durable Conclusions

- The June 2026 exceptional-edge corruption family is fixed in-tree by making HOT `ssa-nomerge` fail closed on `try_table` / throw-family flow, matching the documented SSA v1 normal-flow-only contract.
- The June 2026 default-local branchy-control drift family is fixed in the raw no-write path: reads of never-written body locals are materialized as explicit type defaults across block/loop/if/try_table bodies without invoking HOT SSA.
- The June 2026 final-lane dropped-unreachable-debris drift family is fixed in the same no-write raw path: `drop (unreachable)` / nested dropped-unreachable debris before a hard `unreachable` is collapsed using the existing shared cleanup helper.
- The April `2026-04-10` dead-param-write parity family is now fixed in-tree for `ssa-nomerge`.
- Current source-mode `ssa-nomerge` replay on the checked-in debug CLI artifact completes and validates, but exact normalized/canonical artifact equality is not currently claimed; the 2026-06-14 `[SSANM-008a]` anchor refresh now first-diffs at `defined=108 abs=135` and narrows the huge-function blocker from nine old anchors to six current `large-structured-local-writes` functions (`Func 3536`, `Func 3781`, `Func 3885`, `Func 4119`, `Func 5417`, and `Func 5419`).
- Random compare fuzz is still useful, but it is not sufficient as the only signoff lane for `ssa-nomerge`.
- The 2026-05-07 current-head local-declaration shaping drift family is fixed in-tree: `ssa_destroy` now matches Binaryen temp-local preservation/reuse for unreachable dead `local.tee` value-if carriers without generic lowerer trimming.
- Fresh post-merge reruns on seed `0x51a` stayed clean in both the mixed-generator and `gen-valid` lanes.
- The reduced unreachable compare-carrier slice behind the traced `Func 523` family is now covered in-tree in both lift and pass tests.
- The old traced `Func 523` `writeback-validate:type mismatch` skip is now retired by the focused extracted-function CLI replay test.
- Exact raw-byte parity is still not claimed because Starshine's raw lowering path can still fail closed on artifact-only writeback families, and this follow-up did not rerun a fresh full-artifact traced skip census.
- The non-current subtype/result block-exit edge clusters now have source-backed coverage for `br_on_non_null` tested-payload widening (`ref.i31` to non-null `eqref`, child-to-parent struct/array producers, and child-to-parent `ref.func` producers) and for `br_on_null` prefix-payload widening (`ref.i31` to nullable `eqref`, child-to-parent struct/array producers, and child-to-parent `ref.func` producers); no behavior-code widening was needed beyond the existing raw branch copy lowering, spill helper, and reference matcher.

## Current In-Tree Status

- The implementation lives in `[../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge.mbt)`.
- The analysis bridge toward Binaryen `SSAify.cpp` lives in `[../../../../../src/ir/local_graph.mbt](../../../../../src/ir/local_graph.mbt)`. The 2026-06-13 `[SSA-LG]001` through `[SSA-LG]005` slices add query facts for parameter-entry sources, body-local default-entry sources, defaultability of body-local entry sources, single-source gets, multi-source merge gets, explicit write opcode kind (`local.set` versus `local.tee`), written local ids, influenced get lists, Binaryen-style already-SSA local classification, per-write merge-influence detection, and per-write no-merge freshening eligibility. `[SSANM-002a]` consumes those facts in `SsaNoMergeRewritePlan`; `[SSANM-003a]` makes the observable straight-line raw `local.set` path consume that plan for set/get freshening decisions; `[SSANM-003b]` extends the same planned straight-line path to `local.tee` while preserving tee stack results; `[SSANM-004a]` consumes planned `MaterializeDefault` get decisions for straight-line defaults plus a narrow normal structured-control subset with body-local default reads and other writes; `[SSANM-005a]` / `[SSANM-005b1]` / `[SSANM-005b2]` preserve simple one-arm, both-arm/block-`br_if`, and void-loop direct-`br_if` merge regions as canonical-only LocalGraph plans; `[SSANM-006b2c1]` / `[SSANM-006b2c2]` now extend the same canonical loop-backedge path to branch-free block-decorated void-loop `br_if 0` backedges that previously fell through to HOT SSA destruction; `[SSANM-006b2c3]` / `[SSANM-006b2c4]` keep branch/table-decorated loop-backedge boundaries out of lifted HOT SSA destruction with `structured-loop-backedge-boundary-noop`, keep invalid lowered carriers classified as writeback safety boundaries, and close the structured fallback reroute subtrack; `[SSANM-005c1]` / `[SSANM-005c2]` classify and mutate a narrow mixed fresh/canonical normal `if`/`local.set` family; `[SSANM-005c3a]` extends that mixed path to small supported `local.tee` write sets while preserving tee stack results; `[SSANM-005c3b]` classifies mixed `br_if` early exits as supported by the same planned path while keeping plain `br` and `br_table` fail-closed; and `[SSANM-005c3c]` classifies nested normal `block` / `if` as supported while keeping loops fail-closed. `[SSANM-005b3]` classifies plain `br` and `br_table` multi-source merge regions as fail-closed from the canonical-only and mixed LocalGraph paths, preserving branch/table helper ownership. `[SSANM-006a3b]` and `[SSANM-006a3c]` extend that fail-closed map to ordinary plain `br` / non-mixed `br_if` / ordinary no-value `br_table` local-source exits. `[SSANM-006a3d]` closes the nested-target pass by keeping nested outer-block `br_if` and nested loop-exit `br_if` shapes off planned LocalGraph reasons unless a later owner proves branch-target safety. `[SSANM-007a2]` now locks the real throwing EH category fail-closed, including throwing `try_table` catch/catch-all exits, direct HOT `throw_ref`, legacy catch/rethrow, and delegate terminators; `[SSANM-007a3]` classifies the retained no-throw `try_table` subsets as ordinary normal-flow local-write or typed-control helper work and adds a call-bearing fail-closed contrast. `[SSANM-007b1]` now inventories typed loop-param/result, table, ref/null, and cast-branch helpers as local raw ABI repair surfaces so `[SSANM-007b2]` and `[SSANM-007b3]` can lock them without treating scratch/proxy locals as ordinary no-merge predecessor copies. `[SSANM-007b2]` now adds executable trace/output locks for scalar/reference typed loop-param proxy helpers, no-copy typed-loop no-mutation boundaries, multi-param/single-result store-model helpers, typed-loop `br_table` helpers, and nested loop-target gates. `[SSANM-007b3a]` / `[SSANM-007b3b]` now add shared trace/validation locks for value-carrying `br`, `br_if`, direct `br_table`, and mixed-target `br_table` operands, preserving branch/table opcodes while rejecting ordinary planned structured LocalGraph reasons. `[SSANM-007b3c]` now extends the same trace/validation boundary proof to representative no-copy, copy-needing/prefix, non-null raw-path, and local-tee tested-producer `br_on_null` / `br_on_non_null` exits; `[SSANM-007b3d]` adds the corresponding cast/fail locks for no-copy, divergent-alias, multi-result, multi-param, no-copy loop-target, and copy-needing loop-target `br_on_cast` / `br_on_cast_fail` exits. `[SSANM-006b3]` retires remaining predecessor-copy wording/helper surfaces from ordinary no-merge claims: public summary/help now says `Freshen single-source locals and materialize defaults while preserving merge traffic.`, the retained lifted HOT `ssa_destroy_into_hot(...)` bridge is documented as fallback risk/sibling-SSA surface, and raw branch/table/typed/EH copy-like helpers remain explicit boundaries rather than ordinary no-merge predecessor copies. Huge-function, artifact, and preset work remain open in later `SSANM` slices. `[SSA-FULL]001` first made the sibling full `ssa` name explicit so future full-SSA work could not silently alias to this pass. `[SSA-FULL]002A` added the full-`ssa` merge planner, and `[SSA-FULL]002B` now activates `ssa` only for direct non-merge families while leaving merge-local mutation open.
- The current raw-lowering fixes live in `[../../../../../src/passes/pass_manager.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/pass_manager.mbt)`: dead param writes spill through fresh locals, live straight-line and typed-if param flows stay on the canonical param slot, no-write default-local reads are rewritten through a dedicated recursive default materializer instead of falling back to HOT SSA, no-write dropped-unreachable debris is cleaned before hard `unreachable` tails, concrete `br_on_null` taken edges insert canonical alias copies before exiting over fallthrough overwrites, concrete `br_on_non_null` exits insert canonical alias copies on the non-null taken edge when needed, no-copy `br_on_cast` / `br_on_cast_fail` exits can stay on the raw path, copy-needing non-loop cast exits, including multi-result label targets, lower through scratch source refs plus inner inverse cast-branch blocks so canonical alias copies run only on the taken edge, single-param typed-loop direct scalar `br`, all-current-target, non-current/nested all-loop-target, and source-backed mixed current-loop/enclosing-label `br_table`, no-copy or copy-needing scalar/reference `br_if` backedges, and no-copy or copy-needing nullable-reference `br_on_null` backedges use a void-loop/proxy-value-block scratch lowering, multi-param/no-result and single-result typed-loop direct current-loop `br`, `br_if`, all-current-target and non-current/nested all-loop-target `br_table`, source-backed mixed current-loop/enclosing-label `br_table` in the store model, `local.get`-, `local.tee`-, `ref.null`-, `ref.cast`-, `any.convert_extern`-, `extern.convert_any`-, `ref.i31`-, `ref.func`-, `struct.new_default`-, or `array.new_default`-tested `br_on_null`, `local.get`-, `local.tee`-, `ref.null`-, `ref.cast`-, `ref.i31`-, `ref.func`-, or module-context subtype-compatible direct `struct.new_default` / `array.new_default`-tested `br_on_non_null` (with concrete `ref.func` heap types also admitted into abstract or nominal function supertypes), and cast `br_on_cast` / `br_on_cast_fail` backedges use a scratch-per-param void-loop/store lowering, with `br_on_null` inserting loop-header canonical alias copies only in the null/taken arm, `br_on_non_null` inserting them only in the non-null/taken arm, and cast branches using inverse cast blocks so copies stay branch-local when needed; those direct current-loop backedges may also sit inside branch-bearing nested `loop` bodies when every nested branch still targets the enclosing typed loop, and may coexist with intervening nested void-loop self-target `br` / `br_if` / all-self-target `br_table` control that stays local to that inner loop, while branch-bearing no-exception nested `try_table` bodies are admitted for the scalar proxy, multi-param/no-result, and single-result store-model helper families, and throwing/call-bearing `try_table`, non-void nested loop self-backedges, and nested branches to other labels remain fail-closed; single-reference-param loop-target `br_on_non_null` backedges use the same void-loop/proxy-value-block lowering as loop-target casts, and copy-needing single-reference-param loop-target cast backedges lower through inverse cast blocks that store the cast payload into the loop scratch and run branch-specific canonical alias copies before the void backedge.
- That rule is an in-tree inference from Binaryen `src/passes/SSAify.cpp` `createNewIndexes()` plus direct `wasm-opt --ssa-nomerge` micro-replays on reduced param-write cases.
- The same pass-manager path still rejects per-function writebacks that fail module-aware validation, in addition to the existing `invalid-escape-carrier` and `suspicious-escape-carrier` families.
- The `cmd` package contains a native debug-artifact replay test in `[../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt](../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt)`, and a focused `moon test src/cmd --target native --filter 'run_cmd_with_adapter validates ssa-nomerge on debug artifact'` run is currently green.
- The reduced `Func 523` follow-up now also lives in `[../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift.mbt](../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift.mbt)`, `[../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift_test.mbt](../../../../../src/ir/hot_lift_test.mbt)`, `[../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt)`, and the focused extracted-function CLI replay in `[../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt](../../../../../src/cmd/cmd_wbtest.mbt)`.
- The 2026-06-09 audit added focused `try_table` exceptional-exit, branchy default-local-read, dropped-unreachable-debris, nested param-slot, large structured raw coverage, needed-only branch/label copies, canonical body-local writes, and `Func 4302` carrier-narrowing regressions in `[../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt](../../../../../src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt)`; details and command evidence live in `[../../../raw/research/0722-2026-06-09-ssa-nomerge-exceptional-edge-audit.md](../../../raw/research/0722-2026-06-09-ssa-nomerge-exceptional-edge-audit.md)`.

## Current Signoff State

- 2026-06-16 dedicated GenValid `[SSANM-012c]` unused appended-local compaction: the current smoke sample still showed Starshine carrying local declarations that earlier default/planned/branch composition had made unreachable. This slice does not claim the dedicated profile family is closed: the executable local traffic was already converging, but the final raw result could retain dead appended locals from an intermediate LocalGraph plan. `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now drops unused locals appended by a single planned structured rewrite and, only for `default-local-reads` SSANM results, compacts unused locals added after the original function-local prefix before final null-`throw_ref` debris handling. The guard is deliberately not applied to ordinary structured/br_table scratch families because existing Binaryen-local-budget fixtures still require their declarations. Focused red-first coverage: `ssa-nomerge drops unused appended locals after post-default branch planning` failed at `30` body locals and now requires `<=26`; after the fix focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `457/457`, `moon fmt`, `moon test src/passes` passed `2492/2492`, `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings, full `moon test` passed `5798/5798`, and native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` passed with pre-existing pass-manager warnings. Direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-unused-appended-locals-10000` compared `7093/10000`, normalized `7093`, mismatches `0`, cached Binaryen command failures `20`. Dedicated smoke `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-unused-appended-locals-10000` requested `10000`, compared `58`, normalized `29`, mismatches `29`, command failures `0`; current failures remain raw-size-losing for Starshine (`+17..+36`, sum `+650`) but normalized sizes are equal. Dedicated coverage `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-coverage-unused-appended-locals-10000` requested `10000`, compared `58`, normalized `29`, mismatches `29`, command failures `0`; current failures remain raw-smaller for Starshine (`-28..-6`, sum `-607`) with equal normalized sizes. `[SSANM-012c]` remains open; the smoke raw-size owner is now more likely local/type declaration ordering or remaining local-numbering shape, not just dead appended declarations.

- 2026-06-16 dedicated GenValid `[SSANM-012c]` post-branch default-chain follow-up: the dedicated smoke family still contained an actionable `SSAify(false)` allocation-order gap after default materialization. Binaryen materializes a body-local entry read after ordinary `block; br 0; end`, then freshens the following single-source `local.set` / `local.get` and `local.tee` / `local.get` chain; Starshine had materialized the default but returned before rebuilding LocalGraph over the materialized body, so those writes stayed canonical. `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now composes default materialization with a post-default planned structured LocalGraph rewrite, and the null-throwref debris path applies the same original/default/post-default planning before collapsing local-only EH debris. Focused red-first coverage: `ssa-nomerge freshens post-branch default chains` and `ssa-nomerge preserves dead-tail fresh local declarations before null throw_ref collapse`; `ssa-nomerge redirects if-arm branch copy aliases` now checks that the final fresh tee is not read after branch-copy redirection without depending on the old pre-default local number. Evidence: focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `456/456`; `moon fmt`; `moon test src/passes` passed `2491/2491`; `moon info` passed with three pre-existing GenValid warnings; full `moon test` passed `5797/5797`; native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` passed with pre-existing pass-manager warnings. Direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-postbranch-default-10000` compared `7094/10000`, normalized `7094`, mismatches `0`, cached Binaryen command failures `20`. Dedicated smoke `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-postbranch-default-10000` requested `10000`, compared `58`, normalized `29`, mismatches `29`, command failures `0`; dedicated coverage `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-coverage-postbranch-default-10000` requested `10000`, compared `57`, normalized `29`, mismatches `28`, command failures `0`. This is forward behavior parity for a reduced default/freshening family, not dedicated-profile closeout; `[SSANM-012c]` remains open.

- 2026-06-15 dedicated GenValid `[SSANM-012c]` loop-carried canonical-write narrowing: the post-default/debris coverage sample still showed an actionable under-freshening family, not a proven Starshine win. Binaryen freshens single-source writes before a later loop-carried canonical region even when the same original local participates in the later loop merge; Starshine's analysis-only loop-carried-preserve bit previously kept every write to that local canonical. `src/passes/ssa_nomerge.mbt` now lets the loop-carried canonical override apply only to writes that actually influence a merge get, leaving ordinary single-source prelude writes eligible for the existing LocalGraph freshening rule. Focused regressions: the planner fixture now proves an overwritten pre-loop set freshens while the loop-entry/backedge writes stay canonical, and `ssa-nomerge composes defaults with typed-loop null throw_ref debris` now asserts the pre-loop single-source `local.tee` freshens after debris collapse. Evidence: both tests failed red-first; after the fix `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `454/454`, `moon fmt`, `moon test src/passes` passed `2489/2489`, `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings, full `moon test` passed `5795/5795`, and native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` passed with pre-existing pass-manager warnings. Direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-loop-carried-freshen-10000` compared `7606/10000`, normalized `7606`, mismatches `0`, cached Binaryen command failures `20`. Dedicated smoke `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-loop-carried-freshen-10000` requested `10000`, compared `56`, normalized `28`, mismatches `28`, command failures `0`; dedicated coverage `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-coverage-loop-carried-freshen-10000` requested `10000`, compared `56`, normalized `28`, mismatches `28`, command failures `0`. The prior sample now freshens the pre-loop chain, but remaining dedicated failures still show Binaryen declaring more unused/future locals around the hard-unreachable tail, so this is forward progress rather than `[SSANM-012c]` closeout.

- 2026-06-15 dedicated GenValid `[SSANM-012c]` pre-write/default-debris materialization follow-up: grouped smoke and coverage failures showed actionable LocalGraph output-shape gaps inside the equal-size family. Binaryen materializes body-local entry reads that occur before later writes as `i32.const 0`, including after ordinary `br` / void `br_table`; Starshine previously skipped those rewrites when the local was written anywhere later in the function. A coverage reduction then showed the same default read before a typed self-branching loop and a local-only null-`throw_ref` `try_table` suffix; Starshine collapsed the EH debris but returned before composing LocalGraph default/freshening over the surviving prefix. `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` now uses prefix-seen writes, admits void `br_table` plus otherwise supported `try_table` bodies to the default-materialization scan, and composes collapsed null-throwref debris with LocalGraph planned structured rewriting/default materialization while leaving real exceptional flow fail-closed. Focused regressions: `ssa-nomerge LocalGraph materializes pre-write body defaults`, `ssa-nomerge materializes defaults before null throw_ref debris`, and `ssa-nomerge composes defaults with typed-loop null throw_ref debris`; the pre-write and typed-loop debris tests failed red-first. Evidence after the fix: `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `454/454`; `moon test src/passes` passed `2489/2489`; full `moon test` passed `5795/5795`; `moon fmt`; `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings; native build passed with pre-existing pass-manager warnings; `git diff --check` passed; direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-default-debris-localgraph-10000` compared `7601/10000`, normalized `7601`, mismatches `0`, cached Binaryen command failures `20`. Dedicated smoke `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-default-debris-localgraph-10000` requested `10000`, compared `55`, normalized `28`, mismatches `27`, command failures `0`; dedicated coverage `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-coverage-default-debris-localgraph-10000` requested `10000`, compared `54`, normalized `27`, mismatches `27`, command failures `0`. The repaired coverage sample now carries the default `i32.const 0` and localgraph/debris trace reason, but remaining dedicated failures still have output-shape drift with Starshine declaring fewer locals; this is forward progress, not dedicated-profile closeout, and `[SSANM-012c]` remains open for the broader freshening/merge-local grouping.

- 2026-06-15 dedicated GenValid `[SSANM-011f]` branch-carrier breadth update: the SSA GenValid surface now has explicit feature labels/templates for `ssa-branch-block-alias-copy`, `ssa-nested-enclosing-label-copy`, `ssa-parallel-branch-carrier-copy`, and `ssa-tee-branch-carrier-copy`. Smoke covers the single-carrier branch-block/nested-enclosing alias shape; coverage/stress also cover parallel branch carriers and tee branch carriers. Focused scanner/profile tests passed (`gen_valid_ssa_tests.mbt` `37/37`, `gen_valid_tests.mbt` `74/74`), `moon test src/validate` passed `1605/1605`, `moon test src/fuzz` passed `627/627`, `moon info` passed with the three pre-existing GenValid warnings, and native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` passed with pre-existing pass-manager warnings. Dedicated smoke `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-branchcarrier2-10000` requested `10000`, compared `58`, normalized `29`, and reported `29` raw mismatches with no command/generator/validation failures; all current smoke failures are equal-size (`0` byte delta) with aggregate `+1 local.get` and fewer Starshine locals. Dedicated coverage `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-coverage-branchcarrier2-10000` requested `10000`, compared `58`, normalized `29`, and reported `29` raw mismatches with no command/generator/validation failures; all current coverage failures are likewise equal-size. This broadens GenValid attribution for branch/enclosing-label local-move families but is not closeout; `[SSANM-012c]` remains open for grouping beyond aggregate equal-size metrics plus parity/stress decisions.

- 2026-06-15 dedicated GenValid `[SSANM-012c]` branch-copy follow-up: the smoke `+12` byte mismatch family was classified as an actionable size-losing branch/parallel-copy output-shape gap, not safe validation-only drift. Sample `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-nullthrowfix4-10000/failures/case-000022-gen-valid` copied both `if` arms through fresh locals and a join scratch before copying back to local `1` at an enclosing-label branch; Binaryen writes the branch carrier directly in each arm. The fix redirects branch-adjacent and branch-block alias suffixes into the arm producers when the scratch has no later reads; focused coverage lives in `ssa-nomerge redirects if-arm branch copy aliases`, and the older enclosing-label divergent-alias fixture now locks the Binaryen-shaped direct writes. Evidence: `moon fmt`; focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` `451/451`; `moon test src/passes` `2486/2486`; native build with pre-existing pass-manager warnings; direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-ifbranchblockfix-10000` compared `7603/10000`, normalized `7603`, mismatches `0`, cached Binaryen command failures `20`. Dedicated smoke `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-ifbranchblockfix-10000` still reports `27` raw mismatches out of `54` compared, but every current failure is equal encoded size; dedicated coverage `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-coverage-ifbranchblockfix-10000` reports `28` raw mismatches out of `56` compared, also all equal-size. Agent classification for the inspected remaining profile families is representation-only/no-size-regression, not final profile closeout; `[SSANM-012c]` stays open pending broader grouping and parity/stress profile decisions.

- 2026-06-15 dedicated GenValid `[SSANM-012c]` null-`throw_ref` debris triage: the first coverage/smoke failure family was classified as an actionable size-losing EH/unreachable output-shape gap. Coverage sample `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-coverage-abs6097-branchcopyfix-10000/failures/case-000022-gen-valid` kept a local-only `try_table` ending in `ref.null noexn; throw_ref` and a dead local `get/drop` after a self-branching loop; Binaryen lowered the EH debris to `unreachable`. Starshine was initially `19` bytes larger, then `3` bytes larger after only removing the EH shell, so this was not accepted as safe drift. The fix adds `ssa-nomerge lowers null throw_ref try_table debris to unreachable`, collapses local-only null-`throw_ref` `try_table` debris to `unreachable`, trims unreachable tails, and strips local-only debris between self-branching loops and the resulting hard unreachable. Evidence: focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` `450/450`, `moon test src/passes` `2485/2485`, native `moon build --target native --release src/cmd` with pre-existing warnings, and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-nullthrowfix4-10000` compared `7605/10000` with `7605` normalized matches, `0` mismatches, and `20` cached Binaryen command failures. - 2026-06-14 `[SSANM-009b13a]` multi-param result-loop carrier closeout: the first implementation step preserved a non-void raw result loop for GC-free multi-param single-result typed loops whose current-loop backedges are only plain `br` and whose body has no `try_table`; `ssa-nomerge preserves result loop carrier for multi-param direct br backedges` failed red-first (`437/438`) and then passed (`438/438`). A follow-up then proved the naive tuple/block-carrier path was not a win: `ssa-nomerge leaves tuple carrier disabled without canonical local proof` failed red-first while Starshine emitted a tuple carrier block, and targeted canonicalization showed the shared `wasm-opt --strip-debug` writer added more helper locals for that direct tuple shape. The final policy disables that tuple path and keeps the source-shaped result-loop boundary for this subset. - 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-003b]` LocalGraph straight-line `local.tee` mutation: `src/passes/pass_manager.mbt` no longer diverts straight-line functions containing `local.tee` to the legacy alias heuristic. The raw straight-line path now consumes `SsaNoMergeRewritePlan` for both `local.set` and `local.tee`: planned `Freshen` tee writes allocate the next planned body local and rewrite the tee target to that local, planned canonical tee writes keep the original local, and planned gets still retarget/materialize/keep according to the LocalGraph get decision. Because the rewrite changes only the target of the flat raw tee instruction, the tee stack result remains in place and operand expressions are not duplicated. Focused public-pipeline tests in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` prove LocalGraph-planned trace/output for overwritten root `local.tee` freshening, stack-result preservation through an `i32.add` consumer, final get retargeting, and a folded/effectful tee operand lowered to one call plus one retargeted tee. - 2026-06-13 `[SSANM-002a]` LocalGraph no-merge planner: `src/passes/ssa_nomerge.mbt` now exposes an analysis-only `SsaNoMergeRewritePlan` with per-write `Freshen(new_local)` / `KeepCanonical` decisions and per-get `Retarget(new_local)` / `MaterializeDefault` / `KeepCanonical` decisions. The planner consumes `HotLocalGraph` facts without mutating the function: it allocates fresh future local ids only for explicit `local.set` / `local.tee` writes that `local_graph_write_is_no_merge_freshenable(...)` marks as non-merge, retargets single-source gets only when their source write was freshened, materializes legal body-local default-entry reads, keeps parameter-entry reads canonical, and leaves multi-source merge gets plus merge-feeding writes canonical. - 2026-06-12 problem-1 arbitrary reference-input coverage slice: added executable coverage for the remaining arbitrary multi-instruction reference branch-input breadth without widening unsafe expression scanning. Positive-supported coverage now explicitly distinguishes typed `if` / typed `select` / direct typed producers from unsupported arbitrary expressions. New fail-closed guards cover direct `call` inputs in typed-loop store and non-current block-exit contexts, `br_on_null` and `br_on_non_null` where the current pipeline can preserve a validating output, `local.get; local.get; call $id_ref` with a final raw call, a prefix-payload non-current `br_on_non_null` call input, `struct.new` / `array.new` with operand evaluation, and call-then-`ref.cast` where the broader structured raw gate still refuses the shape. The guard contract is output validation plus raw branch preservation; some shapes reach HOT and are rejected by writeback validation. The current-loop direct-call `br_on_non_null` gap has since been reduced by the single-reference-result call follow-up above, and the no-prefix zero-param non-current `br_on_non_null` direct-call subset has also been admitted; non-current `br_on_null`, explicit-operand/prefix-payload non-current calls, and other arbitrary expression inputs remain guarded or open. - 2026-06-12 sampled debug-artifact local-allocation parity refresh: the saved `.tmp/self-ssa-nomerge-debug-wasi-bronull-prefix-subtype-results` first-diff bucket was refreshed after native artifact generation was unblocked by commit `e0f786434`, then reduced through commits `0dc102965` and `ee4a17d0e`. The `abs=111` typed loop-param shape was a real parity gap: Binaryen lowered the loop-carried scalar through a fresh scratch while Starshine kept the typed loop. That gap is now covered by `ssa-nomerge artifact parity lowers loop-param block-branch scratch` in `src/passes/ssa_nomerge_test.mbt`, and refreshed Starshine output writes the loop-param scratch while keeping Binaryen-like canonical pre-loop/header tees. The residual sampled differences at `abs=95`, `abs=98`, `abs=110`, `abs=111`, and `abs=115` are classified as Starshine-winning differences, not uninspected representation drift: inspected residuals are dominated by Starshine keeping single-use call results on the Wasm operand stack across intervening void calls instead of spilling and immediately reloading extra locals. This is semantically safe because the intervening void calls consume only their explicit operands and cannot observe the lower stack value; if they trap, the spill/local state is unobservable. Refreshed current metrics show smaller canonical print/body text and fewer local writes/gets for every sampled residual: `abs=95` Binaryen `print=140614 body=114259 locals=1090 writes=929 gets=1847 maxref=1089` versus Starshine `print=128849 body=108952 locals=822 writes=819 gets=1741 maxref=821`; `abs=98` Binaryen `18203/14697/140/121/245/139` versus Starshine `17091/13857/126/103/226/125`; `abs=110` Binaryen `28141/22116/247/204/307/246` versus Starshine `26810/21083/232/181/280/231`; `abs=111` Binaryen `6286/4916/51/41/69/50` versus Starshine `6206/4828/49/39/67/48`; and `abs=115` Binaryen `10189/8950/46/37/132/45` versus Starshine `10043/8818/43/34/129/42`. This classification is artifact-sample scoped: it does not claim exact artifact equality, final pass closeout, or that future local-allocation drift can be waved through without the same semantic and measurement evidence.

- 2026-06-12 prefix-payload if-result `br_on_non_null` follow-up: raw structured `ssa-nomerge` now preserves non-current block-exit prefix label payloads when the final tested reference is a trailing single-result `if (result ref)` feeding `br_on_non_null`. The red repro used a block result `(i32, externref)`: the `i32` prefix was already on the stack after spilling the tested ref, and the old synthetic `ref.is_null` / else-branch rewrite failed validation with `writeback-validate:stack underflow`. The fix spills only prefix label results (all label result lanes before the final tested ref) around the synthetic `if`, restores them in the non-null/taken branch before `ref.as_non_null`, and restores them on the null fallthrough so the original fallthrough producer can still supply the final nullable ref. Focused red/green evidence: `ssa-nomerge rewrites non-current prefix if-result br_on_non_null branch inputs` failed before implementation with stack underflow, then focused `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` passed `277/277`, `moon test src/passes` passed `2298/2298`, `moon fmt`, `moon info` passed with the 3 pre-existing GenValid warnings, full `moon test` passed `5573/5573`, native `src/cmd` build passed with pre-existing warnings, and direct compare `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-prefix-if-nonnull-10000` requested `10000`, compared `7606`, had `7606` normalized matches, `0` mismatches, and `20` Binaryen/tool command failures. This is Binaryen behavior Starshine should implement: no raw `br_on_non_null` remains after the effectful typed-`if` producer, and output validates without duplicating branch condition or arm effects. Broader arbitrary multi-instruction inputs, type-indexed/multi-result producers, multi-result typed loops, `try_table`, nested non-void/other-target branches, exact artifact parity, and O4z slot policy remain active.

- 2026-06-11 loop-target cast copy follow-up: raw structured `ssa-nomerge` now admits the next narrow typed loop-param cast backedge subset: typed loops with exactly one reference param and no results, direct current-loop `br_on_cast` / `br_on_cast_fail` backedges, and branch-specific canonical alias copies required before the loop header observes carried locals. ## Coverage / Investigation Lanes

### 2026-06-09 join-allocation investigation (case `000001`)

Reduced block-join replay (`.tmp/ssa-block-join-minimal/`) proves **semantic-equivalent join allocation drift** when both tools actually run `ssa-nomerge`: Starshine’s raw structured path keeps canonical slots (`$x`/`$x`/`$x`) while Binaryen fresh-allocates per set (`$2`/`$3`/`$3`). Both outputs validate and observe the same post-join value.

The dense GenValid `ssa-nomerge` profile smoke lane (`0/100` normalized) is **not** primarily a normalizer gap. For case `000001`, `starshine.raw.wasm` is unchanged from input (`330` bytes, HOT `changed=false`, raw structured rewrite `None`), while Binaryen applies `--ssa-nomerge` (`271` bytes). The harness compares canonicalized **untransformed** Starshine output against Binaryen’s transformed output because the dense template combines fail-closed / raw-skip shapes with rewrite-expected slices in one function (`ssa_nested_cfg_fail_closed_shape`, dropped-increment guard shapes, and combined structured density).

**Classification:** coverage-lane artifact for the dense profile; `semantic-equivalent-join-allocation-drift` only for isolated fixtures where both sides transform.

**Normalizer:** opt-in `--normalize ssa-local-allocation-debris` stays narrow (straight-line islands and immediate pre-`if` carriers only). Do not broaden it across control-flow joins without proof and negative tests.

**Signoff baseline:** mixed-generator `100000` lane with `--normalize local-cleanup-debris` (`99751/99751` normalized matches) under **Current Signoff State** above.

### GenValid profile split (2026-06-09)

| Profile | Purpose | Templates included | Templates excluded |
|---|---|---|---|
| `ssa-nomerge-coverage` (`ssa-nomerge` alias) | Dense SSA body templates, all `ssa-*` coverage floors, fail-closed stress shapes, supported nested `drop(if (result t) ...)` family | straight-line multi-def, tee, param write, if-join, default merge, loop backedge, typed loop-param/backedge fail-closed, `try_table`/`throw_ref` exceptional fail-closed, block join, br_table, parallel-copy (+ cycle), unreachable carrier, dropped increment guarded/reversed, dropped-unreachable debris before hard unreachable, nested-CFG fail-closed, nested result-if straight-line/scalar/condition/arm/mixed templates, structured early-return, block `br`/`br_if`, structured-param merge, branch-local-not-read-later, default-local read after branchy control, canonical body-local next-read, immediate `local.set; br` block exit, enclosing-label copy-before-exit, void br_table canonical copies | — |
| `ssa-nomerge-smoke` | Quick coverage-signal profile for smoke/regression runs that should hit structured SSA branch shapes without dense stress slices | straight-line multi-def, tee, param write (when i32 param), if-join phi, one-arm default merge, structured early-return, block `br`/`br_if`, structured-param merge, branch-local-not-read-later, default-local read after branchy control, canonical body-local next-read, immediate `local.set; br` block exit, enclosing-label copy-before-exit | loop backedge, br_table (including void br_table copy dispatch), parallel-copy, unreachable carrier, dropped increment guarded/reversed, dropped-unreachable debris before hard unreachable, nested-CFG / typed-loop / exceptional fail-closed, dense nested result-if condition/value-block/scalar variants |
| `ssa-nomerge-parity` | Green compare candidate: rewrite shapes where both tools transform without fail-closed skip or structured branch allocation drift | straight-line multi-def, tee, param write (when i32 param), if-join phi, one-arm default merge | loop backedge, block join, br_table, parallel-copy, unreachable carrier, dropped increment guarded/reversed, dropped-unreachable debris, nested-CFG / typed-loop / exceptional fail-closed, nested result-if coverage templates, structured branch smoke shapes, default-local branchy-control, canonical-next-read, immediate set/br, enclosing-label copy-before-exit, and void br_table copy structured slices |
| `ssa-nomerge-stress` | Reserved pathological/fail-closed lane (currently aliases dense coverage templates) | same as coverage (including typed-loop-param, exceptional-flow, and nested result-if templates) | — |

Use `--gen-valid-profile ssa-nomerge-parity` with parity-appropriate `--require-feature` floors for targeted green GenValid parity-profile compare lanes. Use `--gen-valid-profile ssa-nomerge-smoke` when a quick smoke should hit structured branch SSA coverage and tolerate current local-allocation representation drift. Keep `--gen-valid-profile ssa-nomerge-coverage` (or legacy `ssa-nomerge`) for dense scanner/floor coverage only. The broad mixed-generator `100000` lane with `--normalize local-cleanup-debris` remains the primary signoff baseline; a green parity-profile lane is strong targeted evidence, not a replacement for that baseline.

2026-06-09 parity-profile compare (trimmed templates A–E only, `--normalize ssa-local-allocation-debris --normalize local-cleanup-debris`):

- `100/100` compared, `100` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-100-v2`)
- `1000/1000` compared, `1000` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-1000`)
- `10000/10000` compared, `10000` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-10000`)

These lanes are **targeted GenValid SSA parity-profile signoff** for the trimmed template set. They do not replace the broad mixed-generator `99751/100000` signoff baseline above.

The earlier dense-profile smoke (`ssa-nomerge-coverage` with loop/block/br_table/parallel-copy in one function) and the quick `ssa-nomerge-smoke` structured-branch lane remain coverage-lane artifacts, not parity-profile compare lanes, until the compare normalizer or pass output converges for structured control-flow local allocation. Current 2026-06-11 smoke evidence: `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-smoke-profile-100` requested and compared `100/100`, with `0` validation/generator/command failures and `100` expected local-allocation representation mismatches. A later branch-copy narrowing run `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-smoke-branch-copy-100` still compares `100/100` with `100` representation mismatches and no validation/generator/command failures; case `000001` writes the unconditional block-exit `local.set; br` path directly to the canonical merge slot. The local-tee/no-copy-`br_if` slice preserves no-copy `br_if` in the focused fixtures and keeps the paired GenValid parity lane green (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-tee-brif-genvalid-normalized-1000`, `1000` compare-normalized matches, `0` mismatches), while `ssa-nomerge-smoke` remains dirty (`.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-smoke-tee-brif-genvalid-normalized-100`, `100/100` mismatches) because broader structured allocation drift remains. The paired green parity checks `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-profile-100-post-smoke` and `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-branch-copy-100` each compared `100/100` with `100` compare-normalized matches and `0` mismatches.

2026-06-11 deeper GenValid SSA coverage adds positive coverage/stress specimens for the previously scanner-only fail-closed facts: `ssa-typed-loop-param-fail-closed-shape` now comes from a valid typed loop-param/backedge template, and `ssa-exceptional-fail-closed-shape` now comes from a valid `try_table` + `throw_ref` template with local writes. These remain coverage/stress-only and are intentionally excluded from `ssa-nomerge-parity` and `ssa-nomerge-smoke`; they prove generator/scanner/floor coverage, not pass closeout.

2026-06-11 raw structured GenValid widening adds four more facts from the recent pass-behavior slices: `ssa-default-local-read-after-branchy-control`, `ssa-dropped-unreachable-debris-before-hard-unreachable`, `ssa-canonical-body-local-next-read`, and `ssa-immediate-block-exit-canonical-set-br`. Coverage/stress include all four; smoke includes the three quick structured allocation signals and intentionally excludes dropped-unreachable debris; parity remains the conservative A–E set. A later same-day copy-family widening adds `ssa-enclosing-label-copy-before-exit` and `ssa-void-br-table-canonical-copies`; coverage/stress include both, smoke includes only the quick enclosing-label copy signal, and parity still excludes both. The coverage/stress/smoke required-feature compare lanes are intentionally dirty but validate and generate without command failures; the parity profile stayed green at `1000/1000` in `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-parity-new-copy-facts-genvalid-normalized-1000-final`.

2026-06-10 nested result-if GenValid coverage (templates O–W in `gen_valid_ssa.mbt`, feature facts `ssa-nested-result-if-*`):

- New GenValid facts distinguish supported `drop(if (result t) ...)` shapes from `ssa-nested-cfg-fail-closed-shape` (`drop(block (result t) ...)` with local writes).
- `ssa-nested-result-if-supported-shape` means the scanner matched the supported `ssa_simple_drop_result_if_allowed(...)` family: stack-boundary condition-window detection (not whole-function prefix), straight-line or single `block (result i32)` conditions, straight-line / single value-block / void-prefix + final value-block arms, both arms present, and scalar `i32`/`i64`/`f32`/`f64` results only. The scanner is conservative: false negatives are acceptable; false positives are not.
- Templates are wired into `ssa-nomerge-coverage` and `ssa-nomerge-stress` only; `ssa-nomerge-parity` stays on the conservative A–E template set.
- Targeted `--require-feature ssa-nested-result-if-supported-shape` lanes on the dense coverage profile are **coverage smoke**, not parity signoff: they combine rewrite-expected nested result-if slices with fail-closed / join-allocation drift shapes in one function body. A dirty 100-case lane is expected when allocation drift and fail-closed shapes share the same dense body. Post-`bcf4b9199` smoke at `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-nested-result-if-supported-100-post-bcf4` reproduced the expected dirty lane (`100/100` mismatches, `0` command failures) with both tools transforming every case.

### 2026-06-10 large-structured skip extraction (`Func 3668` / `Func 1265`)

Post-bcf4 trace census (`.tmp/ssa-nomerge-post-bcf4-trace/stderr.txt`) had `17` `large-structured-local-writes` skips and `0` `skip-invalid-lower` lines. The smallest skip by scanned instruction count was **`Func 3668`** (`instrs=4509`, `locals=620`); the next-smallest named target was **`Func 1265`** (`instrs=4563`, `locals=614`).

**Classification:** raw structured-path **instruction-count threshold only**. In `run_hot_pipeline_raw_ssa_nomerge` (`pass_manager.mbt`), branch-bearing structured functions skipped when `instr_count > structured_branch_raw_instr_limit` (`4096`) or when `base_local_count > structured_branch_raw_local_limit` (`1024`). Both `Func 3668` and `Func 1265` exceeded the instruction limit only (`4509` / `4563` > `4096`; locals stay well under `1024`). This was not `skip-invalid-lower`, not nested-CFG HOT fail-closed, not typed-loop-param control, and not exceptional flow.

The 2026-06-11 threshold slices raised the branch-bearing structured raw instruction budget to `4608` first, then both the branch-bearing and no-branch structured instruction budgets to `5376`, after synthetic red/green boundary coverage and extracted-artifact validation for sampled functions. Fresh full-artifact trace `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-structured-8192-brtable-trace/stderr.txt` now has `9` `large-structured-local-writes` skips and `0` `skip-invalid-lower` lines. The 2026-06-11 8192-budget follow-up additionally admitted `Func 502` (`7132` / `827`) and `Func 5418` (`7925` / `894`) after red/green synthetic boundary coverage, direct compare, and full-artifact trace validation. Remaining threshold/local-count owners are `Func 265` (`9664` / `1175`), `Func 3518` (`8965` / `1547`), `Func 3536` (`16195` / `2871`), `Func 3781` (`39283` / `6634`), `Func 3885` (`26350` / `3879`), `Func 4119` (`9458` / `1332`), `Func 4522` (`12067` / `976`), `Func 5417` (`19507` / `3524`), and `Func 5419` (`15300` / `2313`).

**Extraction replay:** `--extract-functions=3668` roots a large dependency closure (`.tmp/ssa-nomerge-large-structured-func3668/extracted.wasm`, validates). The rooted function replays as `Func 24` with the same `instrs=4509 locals=620` payload and `large-structured-local-writes` trace. Starshine leaves that function unchanged on the raw fast path; Binaryen `--ssa-nomerge` transforms the extracted module. Self-opt compare on the extracted module validates both sides but is not normalized/canonical equal (`defined=1 abs=25` first diff).

**Reduced fixture:** a programmatic WAT fixture with one `block ... br 0` prefix plus `1030` `if/else` pairs crosses the same threshold (`instrs=4125`, `large-structured-local-writes`); `1020` pairs stay on `structured-local-writes` (`instrs=4085`). Regression tests in `ssa_nomerge_test.mbt` lock that boundary without embedding the 1.5 MB extracted artifact.

**2026-06-14 anchor refresh:** `[SSANM-008a]` supersedes the count in this older extraction note. Current direct traced replay `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-huge-anchor-refresh-20260614` has six `large-structured-local-writes` skips (`Func 3536`, `Func 3781`, `Func 3885`, `Func 4119`, `Func 5417`, and `Func 5419`) and `0` `skip-invalid-lower` lines. The old `Func 265`, `Func 3518`, and `Func 4522` anchors now validate through non-huge boundary/no-op routes in extracted replays.

**Current huge-function follow-up:** `[SSANM-008b]` now records LocalGraph planner counts for the 6 remaining artifact functions plus the 3 drifted non-huge boundaries. Keep the six current huge guards in backlog until `[SSANM-008c]` decides whether to admit a narrow threshold subset and `[SSANM-008d]` measures raw-structured rewrite cost/validation evidence. Do not raise the structured raw instruction/local budgets from a single extracted replay or without preserving direct compare and artifact validation evidence.

## Remaining Gap

- Dropped-local-increment debris no longer triggers a whole-function HOT fail-closed skip. HOT SSA rewrite preserves reaching locals for the exact `drop(i32.add(local.get, i32.const 1))` shape and `local.tee` variants on reduced HOT-path fixtures; reversed operands and non-`1` constants remain validated boundary shapes. Broader integer widths remain unclaimed until tested.
- A tiny nested-CFG subset is now supported on the HOT path: straight-line `drop(block (result t) ...)` value blocks with only local get/set/tee, constants, and simple numeric ops (`ssa_simple_drop_value_block_allowed(...)` plus inline rename in `ssa_local_visit_node`), and straight-line `drop(if (result t) ...)` with a single scalar numeric result (`i32`/`i64`/`f32`/`f64`), both arms present, and a straight-line terminator-free condition with local get/set/tee and simple numeric traffic, or one simple `block (result i32)` condition with the same straight-line local traffic (`ssa_simple_condition_value_block_allowed(...)` / `ssa_simple_result_if_condition_allowed(...)` / `ssa_simple_drop_result_if_allowed(...)` plus CFG-backed rename/use-def inline visits with per-root segment isolation and join phis on the post-`drop` continuation). Condition-local writes are allowed only because CFG keeps branch-free condition blocks in the predecessor block that dominates both arms and rename/use-def visit that block before the arm regions; branches and nested control in the condition stay fail-closed. The dropped result value is not SSA-modeled; arms still need CFG/SSA for local traffic. `v128`, reference/GC, and multi-value result-if remain unsupported. `ssa_nomerge_has_nested_cfg_sensitive_control(...)` still fail-closes all other nested value-control shapes.
- Nested CFG-sensitive behavior remains fail-closed for HOT SSA mutation beyond the supported subsets and is regression-covered: nested result-typed `if` inside dropped value blocks, nested `br` / `br_if` / `loop` / nested `if` inside supported operand shapes, missing-else or multi-value operand `if`, and broader nested control must not produce `pass[ssa-nomerge]:mutated` on the hot path and must leave the hot-path revision unchanged. Root-level value blocks and structured control bodies whose children are region-root slots remain outside this guard and may still rewrite through HOT SSA or the raw no-write path.
- Future work requires nested-region-aware liveness/use-def for unsupported shapes, exact local read discovery inside arbitrary nested value control, rename/destruction for nested `if`/loop/branch shapes, and lowering tests that prove local copies are inserted only at valid stack-neutral sites — not Binaryen parity claims for full nested CFG-sensitive SSA.
- Void loop backedges now have a narrow raw structured subset: void `loop` bodies and void loop-target `br` / `br_table` backedges can rewrite without entering HOT SSA, using loop-header read-before-write facts to preserve loop-carried canonical locals and to freshen only dead loop-local writes. This subset covers the source-backed no-copy loop-target `br_table` and loop-carried read-before-write `br_table` regressions; no-copy loop-target `br_if` is also admitted by the later conditional-backedge slice. Copy-needing conditional loop backedges, result-carrying loop targets, and broader loop-param ABI remain unsupported.
- Typed loop-param control has narrow raw structured exceptions for direct current-loop backedges. No-result single-param loops use the proxy value-block model for scalar and reference branch families; no-result multi-param loops use a scratch-per-param store model for direct `br`, `br_if`, all-current-target `br_table`, and no-copy `br_on_null` whose tested nullable ref is a lowered `local.get`; single-result loops use the same store model plus a synthetic outer result block for direct `br`, `br_if`, all-current-target `br_table`, and the same no-copy `br_on_null` subset. Multi-result typed loops, non-current-loop `br_table` targets, branch-bearing nested `loop` / `try_table` bodies, copy-needing multi-param `br_on_null`, arbitrary-tested `br_on_null`, and broader result-loop/reference `br_on_*` header models remain explicitly unsupported and intentionally fail-closed. HOT represents typed loop params as `BlockResultResolved` param prefixes on `HotOp::Loop` children and as branch operands on backedges, with `HotLabelInfo.branch_arity` recording the payload count. SSA v1's local overlay models only `LocalGet` / `LocalSet` / `LocalTee` reaching definitions; it does not treat loop-param stack flow as local defs, and destruction only inserts predecessor copies for overlay phis on normal CFG edges — not wasm branch operands that re-enter typed loop headers.
- `ssa-nomerge` is safe because typed-loop-param HOT mutation still skips via `ssa_nomerge_has_loop_param_control(...)`; the raw loop-target exceptions are separate, limited to direct current-loop backedges recognized before rewrite, and use stack-neutral or edge-local copy placement before the proxy/store lowering updates loop-param scratches.
- Broader typed-loop-param behavior is fail-closed for HOT SSA mutation and regression-covered: pipeline traces must not contain `pass[ssa-nomerge]:mutated` for unsupported typed-loop-param fixtures, locals written before the loop stay preserved, and backedge-carried param values stay separate from unrelated body locals. The older `br_if` fixture-validation blocker is superseded by the current scalar WAT and concrete-ref programmatic mixed-family fixtures; remaining fail-closed cases are multi-result typed loops, non-current `br_table` targets, branch-bearing nested `loop` / `try_table`, and broader loop-param/header SSA shapes.
- Future work requires loop-param-aware liveness, use-def facts for branch operands, phi placement at typed loop headers, rename semantics that distinguish entry vs backedge param values, destruction copies before loop backedge terminators, lowering that preserves typed loop branch operands for the still-unsupported branch/result shapes, and validated coverage for each widened subset — not broad Binaryen parity claims for typed-loop SSA.
- Exceptional-edge SSA remains explicitly unimplemented and intentionally deferred. The CFG already records `ExceptionalEdge` successors for `try` / `try_table` headers and throw-family terminators, but SSA v1 liveness, dominators, phi placement, dominator-stack rename, and predecessor-copy destruction all follow the normal-flow-only contract.
- Catch continuations are not dominated by throwing blocks.
- The current rename algorithm cannot propagate reaching definitions across exceptional edges without a dedicated exceptional SSA mode.
- `ssa-nomerge` is safe because it skips exceptional-flow HOT mutation via `ssa_nomerge_has_exceptional_flow(...)`, not because the local SSA overlay models exceptional successors.
- Exceptional-flow behavior is fail-closed for HOT SSA mutation and regression-covered: `try_table` write-before-throw, default-local catch continuation, conditional throw with a preceding local write, legacy `rethrow` / `delegate` shapes, and a pipeline trace that must not contain `pass[ssa-nomerge]:mutated`. Some existing raw/no-write normalization may still preserve semantics, but `ssa-nomerge` must not enter HOT local-SSA rewriting for exceptional-flow functions. These tests prove preserved local traffic where writes exist; they do not enable exceptional SSA rewriting.
- Full exceptional SSA remains deferred. Future work requires exceptional-inclusive liveness, catch-block phi placement, exceptional phi inputs, rename semantics for catch blocks, SSA destruction copies before throw/rethrow/delegate terminators, and shape-by-shape guard narrowing with rewrite tests — not Binaryen parity claims for exceptional SSA.
- The O4z public preset still intentionally no-ops `ssa-nomerge`; the direct-pass corruption and debris fixes do not by themselves justify re-enabling the O4z slot.
- The 2026-06-09 direct final lane is normalized-green at `99751/100000` with `0` mismatches, and the param-slot / needed-copy follow-ups stayed green at `9977/10000`; artifact exact parity and O4z neighborhood replay remain open.
- The direct `[SSA]001` temp-local declaration drift is closed by focused tests plus the current `10000 / 10000` `gen-valid` lane.
- The focused extracted-function CLI replay now proves that the old `Func 523` `writeback-validate:type mismatch` skip is retired.
- A fresh direct traced skip census after the large-structured / `Func 4302` follow-up is available in `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-high-threshold-narrow-ssa-trace`, and the post-`bcf4b9199` rerun in `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-post-bcf4-trace` had raw fast/no-op skip families `2524` `structured-local-writes`, `1077` `no-local-writes`, `1020` `straight-line-local-writes`, and `17` `large-structured-local-writes`; there were `0` `skip-invalid-lower` lines. The 2026-06-11 `4608`-instruction budget slice updated the large census to `15`; the later `5376` structured budget slice updated it to `11`, and the high-threshold / no-copy `br_table` follow-up updates it to `9` `large-structured-local-writes` with still `0` `skip-invalid-lower` in `.tmp/ssa-nomerge-structured-8192-brtable-trace`; remaining large skips carry exact payloads such as `func=(Func 3781) instrs=39283 locals=6634`. The older `2026-04-11` count of `228` suspicious skips and the param-slot follow-up count of `1` `Func 4302` suspicious skip are both superseded.
- The same input still succeeds under Binaryen with `wasm-opt tests/node/dist/starshine-debug-wasi.wasm --all-features --ssa-nomerge`.
- So the current output-facing blocker for the reduced `Func 523` family is fixed, the `Func 4302` false-positive suspicious skip is narrowed away, most large-structured direct no-ops are now covered, and the high-threshold raw-structured artifact size regression is fixed by needed-only copies/canonical body-local reuse. Direct artifact replay remains mandatory because exact normalized/canonical function parity is not green. The 2026-06-14 `[SSANM-008a]` refresh supersedes the older `9`-function skip count with six current huge structured functions plus three drifted non-huge boundary/no-op anchors.

## Practical Rule

- Keep direct debug-artifact replay in the `ssa-nomerge` signoff loop.
- Treat the seeded `binaryen-rec-group-zero` wasm-smith failure as an oracle parser gap, not an SSA semantic mismatch.
- Treat current-source behavior parity as green for the fixed dead-param family, the reduced unreachable compare-carrier follow-up, the exceptional-edge fail-closed guard, the raw no-write default-local rewrite, the raw no-write dropped-unreachable-debris cleanup, and the raw structured needed-copy/canonical-local cleanup, but do not claim exact artifact parity until a fresh traced full-artifact replay is normalized/canonical-function equal or the remaining representation drift is intentionally accepted.
- Keep the direct artifact replay and the `10000 / 10000` `gen-valid` compare lane together as the minimum signoff pair; the current `0x5eed` `gen-valid` lane is green in `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-10000-post-bcf4` (supersedes `.tmp/pass-fuzz-ssa-nomerge-genvalid-10000-if-order-fix-rerun`).
